 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc648137_1"></A>PART I </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>INTRODUCTION </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unless
otherwise indicated, all references herein to &#147;Ericsson,&#148; the &#147;Company,&#148; &#147;the Group,&#148; &#147;we,&#148; &#147;us,&#148; or &#147;our&#148; or &#147;our company&#148; are references to Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson and
its consolidated subsidiaries. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This document is our Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> for the year ended
December&nbsp;31, 2017 (the &#147;2017 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F&#148;).</FONT> Reference is made to the English version of our Swedish Annual Report for 2017, with certain adjustments made to comply with U.S. requirements, which is
attached hereto as Exhibit 15.1 (the &#147;2017 Swedish Annual Report&#148;). Only (i)&nbsp;the information included in this 2017 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F,</FONT> (ii)&nbsp;the information in the 2017 Swedish Annual Report that is
incorporated by reference in this 2017 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F,</FONT> and (iii)&nbsp;the exhibits to the 2017 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> that are required to be filed pursuant to the Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> shall be deemed to be filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission for any purpose, including incorporation by reference into the Registration Statement on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">F-3</FONT>
filed on May&nbsp;8, 2015 (File <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">No.&nbsp;333-203977)</FONT> and any other document filed by us pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, which incorporates by reference the 2017 Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F.</FONT> Any information in the 2017 Swedish Annual Report that is not referenced in the 2017 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> or filed as an exhibit thereto shall not be deemed to be so incorporated
by reference. Certain industry, technical and financial terms used in this 2017 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> are defined in the subsections entitled &#147;Glossary&#148; and &#147;Financial Terminology&#148; of the 2017 Swedish
Annual Report, which are incorporate herein by reference. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Market data and certain industry forecasts used herein were obtained from
internal surveys, market research, publicly available information and industry publications. While we believe that market research, publicly available information and industry publications we use are reliable, we have not independently verified
market and industry data from third-party sources. Moreover, while we believe our internal surveys are reliable, they have not been verified by any independent source. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information included on <U>www.ericsson.com</U> and other websites that appear in this 2017 Form
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> is not incorporated by reference herein. From time to time, we may use our website as a channel of distribution of material company information. Financial and other material information regarding our
company is routinely posted on and accessible at <U>www.ericsson.com</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This 2017 Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-F</FONT> includes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">forward-looking</FONT> statements,
including statements reflecting management&#146;s current views relating to the growth of the market, future market conditions, future events, financial condition, and expected operational and financial performance, including, in particular the
following: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Exchange Rates </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following tables provide information with respect to the exchange rate for SEK per USD 1.00 based on the noon buying rate for cable
transfers in SEK as certified for customs purposes by the Federal Reserve Bank of New York. The noon buying rate of 16 March 2018 was SEK 8.1960 per USD 1.00. The average exchange rate is computed using the noon buying rate on the last business day
of each month during the period indicated. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Legal and commercial name of the Parent Company:</B> Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson (publ). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Organization number:</B> 556016-0680 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Legal form of the
Parent Company:</B> A Swedish limited liability company, organized under the Swedish Companies Act. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Country of incorporation:</B> Sweden. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Date of incorporation:</B> The Parent Company was incorporated on August&nbsp;18, 1918, as a result of a merger between AB LM Ericsson&nbsp;&amp; Co. and
Stockholms Allm&auml;nna Telefon AB. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Domicile:</B> Our registered office is Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson, SE&#150;164 83 Stockholm, Sweden. Our
headquarters are located at Torshamnsgatan 21, Kista, Sweden. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Telephone number:</B> +46 10 719 0000 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Website:</B> <U>www.ericsson.com</U>. The information included on our website is not incorporated herein by reference. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Agent in the US:</B> Ericsson Inc., Vice President Legal Affairs, 6300 Legacy Drive, Plano, Texas 75024. Telephone number: +1 972 583 0000. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Shares:</B> Ericsson&#146;s Class&nbsp;A and Class&nbsp;B shares are traded on Nasdaq Stockholm. In the US, our American Depository Shares (ADS), each
representing one underlying Class&nbsp;B share, are traded on NASDAQ New York. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">5 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>

<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Parent company operations:</B> The business of the parent company, Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson, consists
mainly of corporate management, holding company functions and internal banking activities. Our parent company operations also include customer credit management activities performed by Ericsson Credit AB on a commission basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Subsidiaries and associated companies:</B> For a list of our significant subsidiaries, please see &#147;Item 4C. Investments&#148;. In addition to our
joint venture <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ST-Ericsson</FONT> (up until August&nbsp;2, 2013), we are engaged in a number of minor joint ventures and cooperative arrangements. For more information regarding risks associated with joint ventures,
strategic alliances and third-party agreements, please see &#147;Item 3D. Financials&#150;Risk Factors - Market, Technology and Business Risks&#148;. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Company history and development </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Innovating to
empower people, business and society </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our origins date back to 1876 when Alexander Graham Bell filed a patent application in the United
States for the telephone. The same year, Lars Magnus Ericsson opened a small workshop in Stockholm to repair telegraph instruments and sell his own telephone equipment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Today, Ericsson enables communications service providers to capture the full value of connectivity. The company&#146;s portfolio spans
Networks, Digital Services, Managed Services, and Emerging Business and is designed to help our customers go digital, increase efficiency and find new revenue streams. Ericsson&#146;s investments in innovation have delivered the benefits of
telephony and mobile broadband to billions of people around the world. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Corporate Governance </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Corporate Governance report 2017 </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="27%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Regulation and compliance </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Sustainability </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Sustainability and corporate responsibility </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sustainability and corporate responsibility are integrated into
Ericsson&#146;s business processes and the Company&#146;s commitment to the triple bottom line of responsible environmental performance and social and economic development is made clear to its stakeholders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson&#146;s ambition is to be a responsible and relevant driver of positive change in society. Ericsson is committed to creating business
value while reducing risk related to environmental, social, employee, human rights, corruption and bribery matters. Ericsson&#146;s sustainability and corporate responsibility performance is regularly measured, assessed and assured. Group policies
and directives have been implemented to ensure consistency across global operations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson&#146;s principal risks relating to
sustainability and corporate responsibility are identified in Ericsson&#146;s risk management framework. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board of Directors is
briefed on sustainability and corporate responsibility issues regularly, or as needed on an ad hoc basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2017, the Chief
Sustainability&nbsp;&amp; Public Affairs Officer was a member of Ericsson&#146;s Executive Team and reported to the President and CEO, and was responsible for handling the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT> management of
Ericsson&#146;s sustainability and corporate responsibility agenda. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Governance and policies </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Responsible business practices are embedded in Ericsson&#146;s
operations to prevent, mitigate and adapt to risks. The Ericsson Group Management System (EGMS) includes policies, processes and directives encompassing responsible sourcing, occupational health and safety, environmental management, anti-corruption
and human rights, for example. External assurance providers audit the EGMS. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Some of the Group Policies and Directives that are of
particular relevance from a sustainability and corporate responsibility perspective are the Code of Business Ethics, the Code of Conduct, the Sustainability Policy, the Occu-pational Health and Safety Policy, the Electro-magnetic Fields and Health
Policy, the Sales Compliance Policy and the Anti-corruption Group Directive, which reflect how Ericsson shall work to secure responsible business practices. These policies and practices are reinforced by employee awareness training and monitoring.
Compliance to Group Policies are mandatory for all employees and operations unless a deviation is approved by the CEO. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Code of Business Ethics </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Code of Business Ethics sets the tone for how Ericsson conducts business globally, and is a guiding framework to support everyone performing work for
Ericsson. The Code of Business Ethics is periodically reviewed and acknowledged by employees and has been translated into more than 30 languages to ensure that it is accessible to all employees and stakeholders. During 2017, 99% of active employees
acknowledged that they have read and understood the Code of Business Ethics. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Employees are encouraged to report any conduct that they believe, in good faith, to be a
violation of laws or the Code of Business Ethics. Ericsson provides employees and external stakeholders with a dedicated communication channel, called the Ericsson Compliance Line, for the reporting of serious compliance concerns involving group or
local management and which relates to; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">a) corruption or fraud </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">b) questionable accounting or auditing matters </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">c) other
matters that might seriously affect the vital interest of Ericsson or personal health and safety. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The process around reporting of violations has been
strengthened and further developed to include both centrally and locally reported allegations of violations in 2017. For this reason there is a significantly higher number of reports in 2017 in comparison with 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During 2017 the Company received 412 cases reported through Ericsson&#146;s whistle-blower tool, the Ericsson Compliance Line. This tool is
available via phone or secure website, 24/7, 365 days a year, and is available in </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">188 countries and in over 75 languages. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reported violations are handled by Ericsson&#146;s Group Compliance Forum, which consists of representatives from Ericsson&#146;s internal audit function,
Group Function Legal Affairs, Group Security, and Group Function Human Resources. The Forum briefs the Audit Committee about all reported violations, providing them with the incident category, a description of the alleged violation, and information
about the decision and outcome. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Code of Conduct </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson&#146;s Code of Conduct applies to employees and suppliers and is based on the UN Global Compact ten principles on human rights, labor conditions,
environmental management and anti-corruption. Ericsson is also committed to implementing the UN Guiding Principles on Business and Human Rights across its business operations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Suppliers must comply with Ericsson&#146;s Code of Conduct requirements. The Company uses a risk-based approach to assess compliance with the
Code of Conduct requirements as part of supplier agreements. The Company has a strong focus on risk mitigation, targeting high-risk portfolio areas and high-risk markets. For prioritized areas such as road and vehicle safety, working at heights,
working hours and labor rights, Ericsson performs regular audits and works with suppliers to ensure measurable and continuous improvements, and has also introduced consequence management. Findings are followed up to ensure that improvements are
made. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Since 2017, the Ethics and Compliance Board &#150; comprised of several members of the Executive Team and chaired by the CEO &#150;
has been responsible to oversee the overall governance of compliance within the Group. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Sustainability risk management </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sustainability risks are defined according to short-term and long-term
perspectives. They are related to long-term objectives as per the strategic direction as well as short-term objectives for the coming year. According to Ericsson&#146;s risk framework, sustainability risks are categorized into industry and market
risks, commercial risks, operational risks and compliance risks. The Company follow its risk management principles, which apply across all business activities, to manage sustainability risks. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Materiality assessment is a central component of the Company&#146;s sustainability and corporate responsibility strategy, target setting,
risks and opportunities management, and reporting process related to its impact on society and environment. Ericsson considers a wide range of economic, environmental and social impacts significant to the business, or which substantively influence
the views and decisions of our key stakeholders. Since 2012, the Company has used a materiality assessment to review significant issues on an annual basis, taking into account emerging trends, stakeholder feedback and other input. Adjustments are
made as needed to incorporate critical issues as they arise. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Group Function Sustainability and Public Affairs coordinates management
of certain sustainability risks, such as occupational health and safety, human rights, and environmental related risks. Risks related to corruption are coordinated by Group Function Legal Affairs, and diversity issues are coordinated by Group
Function Human Resources. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For information on risks that could impact the fulfillment of targets and form the basis for mitigating
activities, see the Swedish Annual Report 2017, Note C20 &#147;Financial risk management and financial instruments&#148; and the Risk Factors section in the Board of Directors&#146; report in the Swedish Annual Report 2017. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">8 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Anti-corruption </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Corruption carries serious legal and reputational risks; impedes business growth; damages
relations with staff, customers, shareholders, suppliers and society as a whole; and is a considerable obstacle to economic and social development in countries around the world. With customers in 180 countries, many of which are considered to be
exposed to a high risk of corruption, prevention and accountability are paramount for Ericsson. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson has a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">zero-tolerance</FONT> approach to corruption expressed in the Company&#146;s Code of Business Ethics. The Company has embedded this guiding principle at its highest levels and implemented it throughout its global
organization with a set of policies and processes. This includes an anti-corruption directive with more detailed guidelines, for example about appropriate levels of gifts and entertainment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#146;s anti-corruption program, focusing on prevention and accountability, is headed by a Chief Compliance Officer, who since
October 2017 reports directly to the Audit Committee of the Board of Directors. The Audit Committee also reviews and evaluates the program at least annually. Further, since 2016, an Ethics and Compliance Board, comprised of several members of the
Executive Team and chaired by the CEO, has been responsible for the overall governance of compliance within the Group. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During
2016&#150;2017 we invited external experts to evaluate the robustness of our anti-corruption program. Following the review, we adjusted the anti-corruption program to closer align with the US Foreign Corrupt Practices Act (FCPA). In 2017, the
program was strengthened with adding resources on group level and appointing Regional Compliance Officers in all Market Areas. Moreover, one of the elements of the Group targets for sustainability and corporate responsibility is anti-corruption.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2017 the Company continued to roll out an automated anti-corruption screening tool for supplier and third party due diligence, which
was launched in 2016. By the end of 2017, close to 93% of active employees had completed the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">anti-corruption</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-learning</FONT> course since the training was
launched in 2013. A customized online anti-corruption training is also available for Ericsson&#146;s suppliers on the Company website. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In
2017, Ericsson introduced a vetting process that focuses on ethics and compliance. So far we have used it for appointments to the Executive Team and for approximately 110 employees in exposed positions. All members of the current Executive Team have
been vetted, and all future recruitments to these positions will also go through mandatory vetting. Business Partner Review Boards have been established in all Market Areas to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">over-see</FONT> mitigation of the
corruption risks in relation to onboarding of new business partners. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson is currently voluntarily cooperating with inquiries from
the United States Securities and Exchange Commission and the United States Department of Justice regarding its compliance with the U.S. Foreign Corrupt Practices Act. As of today, these inquiries concern a period from January&nbsp;1, 2007 and
onwards, and the Company will make additional disclosures regarding these inquiries to the extent required. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Disclosure pursuant to Section&nbsp;219
of the Iran Threat Reduction and Syria Human Rights Act of 2012 (ITRA) </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson has conducted business in Iran/Persia since the late nineteenth
century, opened an office in Iran in 1973 and later established a local subsidiary in the country. Ericsson strongly believes in enabling communication for all and believes that access to communications can enable the right to health, education and
freedom of expression. Ericsson&#146;s business activities in Iran principally involve the sale of communications infrastructure related products and services, including support, installation and maintenance services. Ericsson&#146;s exports from
the European Union (the &#147;EU&#148;) to Iran are performed under export licenses from the Swedish Agency for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Proliferation</FONT> and Export Controls. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Due to its operations in Iran, and having staff permanently in the country, Ericsson has contacts with its local customers and retains certain local
suppliers, including banks, and service providers. In addition, Ericsson has other dealings incidental to its local activities, such as making payments for taxes, salaries, rents, utilities and office and similar supplies as well for local
accommodation and transportation and customs related services. As a result, Ericsson has contact with companies and public functions that may be owned or controlled by the government of Iran. While Ericsson seeks to obtain information regarding the
actual business names and ownership of customers and other counterparties in Iran through its policies and procedures designed to ensure that Ericsson &#147;knows its customers&#148;, it is difficult to determine ownership and control with
certainty, particularly with respect to determining whether an entity engaged in commercial activities is owned or controlled by the government. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During 2017, Ericsson sold communications infrastructure related products and services in Iran to the following
telecommunications companies operating in the country: Farabord Dadehavare Iranian (&#147;Farabord&#148;), Hiweb, Mobile Communication Company of Iran (&#147;MCCI&#148;), MTNIrancell and Pars Online. During 2017, Ericsson and Telecommunications
Company of Iran (&#147;TCI&#148;) has had discussions relating to potential future such sales by Ericsson to TCI. During 2017, Ericsson&#146;s gross revenue (reported as net sales) related to sales to Farabord, Hiweb, MCCI and MTNIrancell and Pars
Online in Iran was approximately SEK 1,945&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson does not normally allocate net profit (reported as net income) on a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">country-by-country</FONT></FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">activity-by-activity</FONT></FONT> basis, other than as set forth in Ericsson&#146;s
consolidated financial statements prepared in accordance with IFRS as issued by the IASB. However, Ericsson has estimated that its operating income (income before taxes and financial net) from such sales, after internal cost allocation was
approximately SEK <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">-117&nbsp;million</FONT> during 2017. Ericsson intends to continue to engage with existing customers and explore opportunities with new customers in Iran while continuously monitoring international
developments as they relate to Iran and its government. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In some instances, Ericsson has had to arrange performance bonds or similar financial guarantees
to secure Ericsson&#146;s performance of obligations under the commercial agreements Ericsson has entered into relating to the business in Iran. In such instances, Ericsson usually engages its banks outside Iran, who in turn engage local banks in
the country. These local banks include Bank Mellat, Tejarat Bank, Melli Bank and Saderat Bank. Although some bonds and guarantees are still in place, no new performance bonds or similar guarantees involving these four banks with respect to
Ericsson&#146;s business activities in Iran were issued during 2017, nor were payments made to beneficiaries under any such existing bond or guarantee during 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During 2017, Maskan Bank, Post Bank of Iran and Tejarat Bank (local banks in Iran) issued bank guarantees to secure Iranian customer payment obligations to
Ericsson. Further, some payments made to Ericsson&#146;s local subsidiary and payments required to be made by the local subsidiary to suppliers involve banks that may be controlled by the government of Iran. Ericsson also received payments from
customers to Ericsson&#146;s accounts outside Iran. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

and indirectly by our parent company as of December&nbsp;31, 2017. A complete list of shareholdings, prepared in accordance with the Swedish Annual Accounts Act and filed with the Swedish Companies Registration Office (Bolagsverket), may be obtained
upon request to: Telefonaktiebolaget LM Ericsson, External Reporting, SE-164 83 Stockholm, Sweden. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Shares owned directly by the Parent

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Sustainability and corporate responsibility </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sustainability and corporate responsibility are integrated into
Ericsson&#146;s business processes and the Company&#146;s commitment to the triple bottom line of responsible environmental performance and social and economic development is made clear to its stakeholders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson&#146;s ambition is to be a responsible and relevant driver of positive change in society. Ericsson is committed to creating business
value while reducing risk related to environmental, social, employee, human rights, corruption and bribery matters. Ericsson&#146;s sustainability and corporate responsibility performance is regularly measured, assessed and assured. Group policies
and directives have been implemented to ensure consistency across global operations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson&#146;s principal risks relating to
sustainability and corporate responsibility are identified in Ericsson&#146;s risk management framework. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board of Directors is
briefed on sustainability and corporate responsibility issues regularly, or as needed on an ad hoc basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2017, the Chief
Sustainability&nbsp;&amp; Public Affairs Officer was a member of Ericsson&#146;s Executive Team and reported to the President and CEO, and was responsible for handling the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT> management of
Ericsson&#146;s sustainability and corporate responsibility agenda. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Governance and policies </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Responsible business practices are embedded in Ericsson&#146;s operations to prevent,
mitigate and adapt to risks. The Ericsson Group Management System (EGMS) includes policies, processes and directives encompassing responsible sourcing, occupational health and safety, environmental management, anti-corruption and human rights, for
example. External assurance providers audit the EGMS. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Some of the Group Policies and Directives that are of particular relevance from a
sustainability and corporate responsibility perspective are the Code of Business Ethics, the Code of Conduct, the Sustainability Policy, the Occupational Health and Safety Policy, the Electro-magnetic Fields and Health Policy, the Sales Compliance
Policy and the Anti-corruption Group Directive, which reflect how Ericsson shall work to secure responsible business practices. These policies and practices are reinforced by employee awareness training and monitoring. Compliance to Group Policies
are mandatory for all employees and operations unless a deviation is approved by the CEO. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Code of Business Ethics </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Code of Business Ethics sets the tone for how Ericsson conducts business globally, and is a guiding framework to support everyone performing work for
Ericsson. The Code of Business Ethics is periodically reviewed and acknowledged by employees and has been translated into more than 30 languages to ensure that it is accessible to all employees and stakeholders. During 2017, 99% of active employees
acknowledged that they have read and understood the Code of Business Ethics. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Employees are encouraged to report any conduct that they believe, in good faith, to be a
violation of laws or the Code of Business Ethics. Ericsson provides employees and external stakeholders with a dedicated communication channel, called the Ericsson Compliance Line, for the reporting of serious compliance concerns involving group or
local management and which relates to; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">a) corruption or fraud </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">b) questionable accounting or auditing matters </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">c) other
matters that might seriously affect the vital interest of Ericsson or personal health and safety. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The process around reporting of violations has been
strengthened and further developed to include both centrally and locally reported allegations of violations in 2017. For this reason there is a significantly higher number of reports in 2017 in comparison with 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During 2017 the Company received 412 cases reported through Ericsson&#146;s whistle-blower tool, the Ericsson Compliance Line. This tool is
available via phone or secure website, 24/7, 365 days a year, and is available in </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">188 countries and in over 75 languages. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reported violations are handled by Ericsson&#146;s Group Compliance Forum, which consists of representatives from Ericsson&#146;s internal audit function,
Group Function Legal Affairs, Group Security, and Group Function Human Resources. The Forum briefs the Audit Committee about all reported violations, providing them with the incident category, a description of the alleged violation, and information
about the decision and outcome. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Code of Conduct </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson&#146;s Code of Conduct applies to employees and suppliers and is based on the UN Global Compact ten principles on human rights, labor conditions,
environmental management and anti-corruption. Ericsson is also committed to implementing the UN Guiding Principles on Business and Human Rights across its business operations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Suppliers must comply with Ericsson&#146;s Code of Conduct requirements. The Company uses a risk-based approach to assess compliance with the
Code of Conduct requirements as part of supplier agreements. The Company has a strong focus on risk mitigation, targeting high-risk portfolio areas and high-risk markets. For prioritized areas such as road and vehicle safety, working at heights,
working hours and labor rights, Ericsson performs regular audits and works with suppliers to ensure measurable and continuous improvements, and has also introduced consequence management. Findings are followed up to ensure that improvements are
made. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Since 2017, the Ethics and Compliance Board &#150; comprised of several members of the Executive Team and chaired by the CEO &#150;
has been responsible to oversee the overall governance of compliance within the Group. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Sustainability risk management </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sustainability risks are defined according to short-term and long-term
perspectives. They are related to long-term objectives as per the strategic direction as well as short-term objectives for the coming year. According to Ericsson&#146;s risk framework, sustainability risks are categorized into industry and market
risks, commercial risks, operational risks and compliance risks. The Company follow its risk management principles, which apply across all business activities, to manage sustainability risks. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Materiality assessment is a central component of the Company&#146;s sustainability and corporate responsibility strategy, target setting,
risks and opportunities management, and reporting process related to its impact on society and environment. Ericsson considers a wide range of economic, environmental and social impacts significant to the business, or which substantively influence
the views and decisions of our key stakeholders. Since 2012, the Company has used a materiality assessment to review significant issues on an annual basis, taking into account emerging trends, stakeholder feedback and other input. Adjustments are
made as needed to incorporate critical issues as they arise. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Group Function Sustainability and Public Affairs coordinates management
of certain sustainability risks, such as occupational health and safety, human rights, and environmental related risks. Risks related to corruption are coordinated by Group Function Legal Affairs, and diversity issues are coordinated by Group
Function Human Resources. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For information on risks that could impact the fulfillment of targets and form the basis for mitigating
activities, see the Swedish Annual Report 2017, Note C20 &#147;Financial risk management and financial instruments&#148; and the Risk Factors section in the Board of Directors&#146; report in the Swedish Annual Report 2017. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Anti-corruption </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Corruption carries serious legal and reputational risks; impedes business growth; damages
relations with staff, customers, shareholders, suppliers and society as a whole; and is a considerable obstacle to economic and social development in countries around the world. With customers in 180 countries, many of which are considered to be
exposed to a high risk of corruption, prevention and accountability are paramount for Ericsson. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson has a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">zero-tolerance</FONT> approach to corruption expressed in the Company&#146;s Code of Business Ethics. The Company has embedded this guiding principle at its highest levels and implemented it throughout its global
organization with a set of policies and processes. This includes an anti-corruption directive with more detailed guidelines, for example about appropriate levels of gifts and entertainment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#146;s anti-corruption program, focusing on prevention and accountability, is headed by a Chief Compliance Officer, who since
October 2017 reports directly to the Audit Committee of the Board of Directors. The Audit Committee also reviews and evaluates the program at least annually. Further, since 2016, an Ethics and Compliance Board, comprised of several members of the
Executive Team and chaired by the CEO, has been responsible for the overall governance of compliance within the Group. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During
2016&#150;2017 we invited external experts to evaluate the robustness of our anti-corruption program. Following the review, we adjusted the anti-corruption program to closer align with the US Foreign Corrupt Practices Act (FCPA). In 2017, the
program was strengthened with adding resources on group level and appointing Regional Compliance Officers in all Market Areas. Moreover, one of the elements of the Group targets for sustainability and corporate responsibility is anti-corruption.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2017 the Company continued to roll out an automated anti-corruption screening tool for supplier and third party due diligence, which
was launched in 2016. By the end of 2017, close to 93% of active employees had completed the Company&#146;s anti-corruption <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-learning</FONT> course since the training was launched in 2013. A customized online anti-
corruption training is also available for Ericsson&#146;s suppliers on the Company website. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2017, Ericsson introduced a vetting
process that focuses on ethics and compliance. So far we have used it for appointments to the Executive Team and for approximately 110 employees in exposed positions. All members of the current Executive Team have been vetted, and all future
recruitments to these positions will also go through mandatory vetting. Business Partner Review Boards have been established in all Market Areas to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">over-see</FONT> mitigation of the corruption risks in relation to
onboarding of new business partners. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson is currently voluntarily cooperating with inquiries from the United States Securities and
Exchange Commission and the United States Department of Justice regarding its compliance with the U.S. Foreign Corrupt Practices Act. As of today, these inquiries concern a period from January&nbsp;1, 2007 and onwards, and the Company will make
additional disclosures regarding these inquiries to the extent required. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Primary manufacturing and assembly facilities </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We continuously adjust our production capacity to meet expected customer demand. During 2017, our overall capacity utilization was around 85%.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The table below summarizes where we have major sites and the total floor space at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end.</FONT>
Facilities are leased. The majority of the floor space within our production facilities is used for assembly. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Note C20 &#150; Financial risk management and financial instruments &#150; Foreign exchange risk </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="18%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Risk Factors </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="27%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Market, technology and business risks </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="27%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Regulatory, Compliance and Corporate Governance risks </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Operating results for the years ended
December&nbsp;31, 2015 and 2016 </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reporting structure in 2016 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Starting July&nbsp;1, 2016, Ericsson implemented an organizational change. The financial reporting during 2016 has been carried out according
to the same segment structure as in 2015; Networks, Global Services and Support Solutions. The 2016 reporting structure is appliedbelow. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">From January&nbsp;1, 2017, financial reporting is done according to the new structure, i.e., by the new segments Networks, IT&nbsp;&amp; Cloud
and Media. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Full-year highlights<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&nbsp;</SUP> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reported sales decreased by &#150;10% mainly due to weaker demand for mobile broadband, especially in markets with a weak macroeconomic
environment. IPR licensing revenues declined to SEK&nbsp;10.0 (14.4) billion.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income declined to SEK 6.3 (21.8) billion due to
lower sales and a changed business mix in mobile broadband, with a lower proportion of capacity business. This was partly offset by lower operating expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash flow from operating activities was SEK 14.0 (20.6) billion. Net&nbsp;cash at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> was SEK
31.2&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board of Directors proposes a dividend for 2016 of SEK 1.00 (3.70) per share to the AGM. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business in 2016 </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In 2016, net sales
decreased by &#150;10% mainly due to lower demand for mobile broadband, especially in markets with a weak macroeconomic environment. Sales declined in all three segments. Both operating income and margin decreased compared to last year due to lower
sales and lower gross margin, partly offset by lower operating expenses.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">IPR licensing revenues were SEK 10.0 (14.4) billion. IPR
licensing revenues in 2015 were positively impacted by a global patent license agreement signed with Apple, which included an initial payment.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Full-year sales for the targeted growth areas; IP network, Cloud, OSS and BSS, TV and Media as well as Industry and Society, were flat and
accounted for 20% of group sales.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The global cost and efficiency program, first initiated in November 2014, and expanded in 2016,
-progressed according to plan. The target of the program is to reduce the annual run rate of operating expenses, excluding restructuring charges, to SEK 53&nbsp;billion in the second half of 2017. Operating expenses in 2016 decreased to
SEK&nbsp;60.5 (64.1) billion which included restructuring charges of SEK &#150;4.1 (&#150;2.8) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ericsson delivered a full-year
cash flow from operating activities of SEK 14.0 (20.6) billion, exceeding the 70% cash conversion target.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial highlights<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&nbsp;</SUP> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Net sales</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reported sales decreased by &#150;10% mainly due to lower demand for mobile broadband, especially in markets with a weak macroeconomic
environment. Sales in Europe declined following completion of mobile broadband projects in 2015. Mobile broadband sales in North America remained stable while Professional Services sales declined, mainly due to lower managed services activities. A
significant managed services contract in North America was renewed with reduced scope. Sales in South East Asia increased, driven by large deliveries in coverage&nbsp;projects. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">IPR licensing revenues amounted to SEK 10.0 (14.4) billion. Sales in 2015 were positively impacted by a global patent license agreement signed
with Apple, which included an initial payment. The baseline for current IPR licensing contract portfolio is approximately SEK 7&nbsp;billion on an annual basis. Smartphone volume growth, agreements with currently unlicensed handset suppliers and IoT
licensing will determine growth opportunities going forward. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Currency exchange rates had no material impact on full-year sales. Sales,
adjusted for comparable units and currency, decreased by&nbsp;&#150;10%. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Full-year sales for targeted growth areas were flat and accounted for 20% of group sales. The
partnership with Cisco has to date generated more than 100 deals across all regions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The sales mix by commodity was: software 22% (23%),
hardware 33% (34%) and services 45% (43%).</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Gross margin </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross margin declined to 29.8% (34.8%) due to a sales mix with lower share of mobile capacity business, higher share of Global Services sales
and lower IPR licensing revenues as well as lower Global Services margins. In addition, restructuring charges included in the gross -margin increased to SEK &#150;3.5 (&#150;2.3) billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Restructuring charges and efficiency program</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges amounted to SEK &#150;7.6 (&#150;5.0) billion. The charges were mainly related to the cost and efficiency program
initially announced in November 2014, and expanded in 2016. The cost and efficiency program is progressing according to plan and the target is to reduce the annual run rate of operating expenses, excluding restructuring charges, to SEK
53&nbsp;billion in the second half of 2017. Efforts continue in order to reduce cost of sales, targeting to improve gross margin in the second half of 2017 compared with full-year 2016. With current plans, total restructuring charges for 2017 are
estimated to be SEK&nbsp;3&nbsp;billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Operating expenses </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total operating expenses decreased to SEK 60.5 (64.1) billion as a result of the cost and -efficiency program and lower amortizations of
intangible assets. Operating expenses included restructuring charges of SEK &#150;4.1 (&#150;2.8) billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Other operating income and expenses</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Other operating income and expenses were SEK&nbsp;0.4 (0.2) billion. Currency hedge contract effects impacted the result with SEK &#150;0.9
(&#150;1.1) billion. They derive from the hedge contract -balance in USD. The SEK has weakened against&nbsp;the USD between December&nbsp;31, 2015 (SEK/USD rate 8.40) and December&nbsp;31, 2016 (SEK/USD rate 9.06). The negative currency hedge
effects were more than offset by several minor positive items.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Operating income </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income decreased to SEK 6.3 (21.8) billion due to lower sales and lower gross margin, partly offset by lower operating expenses.
Operating margin was 2.8% (8.8%). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial net </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The financial net declined to SEK &#150;2.3 (&#150;1.9) -billion following decreased interest rates and depreciated local currencies in certain
markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Taxes</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Tax cost decreased to
SEK &#150;2.1 (&#150;6.2) billion due to lower net income, offset by prior-year adjustments and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-deductible</FONT> expenses. These factors resulted in a tax rate of 53% in 2016 compared with the more normal tax
rate of 31% in 2015. Average tax rate for the years 2011&#150;2015 was&nbsp;32%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Net income and EPS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income decreased to SEK 1.9 (13.7) billion., for the same reasons as for the decrease in operating income. EPS diluted was SEK 0.52 (4.13)
and EPS <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(Non-IFRS)</FONT> was SEK 2.66 (6.06). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business results &#150; Segments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Networks </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Background </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Networks represented 48.7% of net sales in 2016 (50.1% in 2015), The segment delivers products and solutions that are needed for mobile and
fixed communication, several generations of radio networks, IP and transmission networks, core networks and cloud. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Business in 2016 </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales as reported decreased by &#150;12%. The decrease was mainly due to lower sales of mobile broadband, reduced sales of core networks and
lower IPR licensing revenues. Core networks sales declined due to lower sales of legacy products, not offset by growth of the new&nbsp;portfolio.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mobile broadband investments were negatively impacted by a weak macroeconomic environment in a number of markets such as Latin America, the
Middle East and South Africa. In addition, sales declined in Europe following the completion of large coverage projects in 2015 and in India due to delayed spectrum auctions. The sales decline was partly offset by sales growth in South East Asia
where large deliveries in mobile broadband coverage projects were made. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">18 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In North America and in North East Asia, investments in network equipment were stable. In
Mainland China, large-scale LTE deployments continued for the third consecutive year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales, adjusted for comparable units and -currency,
decreased by &#150;13%. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income and margin decreased, mainly due to a lower share of mobile broadband capacity sales and lower
IPR licensing revenues. The decrease was partly offset by reduced operating expenses, mainly as an effect of the ongoing cost and efficiency program. The work to improve profitability continued with significant headcount reductions and structural
changes. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges amounted to SEK &#150;4.0 (&#150;2.8) billion and the negative effect from currency hedge contracts was
SEK &#150;0.7 (&#150;0.9) billion.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Global Services </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Background </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Global Services represented
45.7% of net sales in 2016 (43.7% in 2015). The segment delivers network rollout services and professional services (i.e., managed services, consulting and systems integration (CSI), customer support as well as network design and optimization
services). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Business in 2016 </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales
as reported decreased by &#150;6%. Professional Services sales declined due to lower managed services activities in North America where a contract has been renewed with reduced scope. CDMA sales declined YoY impacting -Professional Services sales
negatively. Network Rollout sales declined due to lower mobile broadband demand, primarily in Europe and Latin America. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales, adjusted
for comparable units and -currency, decreased by &#150;5%.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Global Services operating income decreased to SEK 3.3 (8.2) billion. Activities
were performed to adapt the service delivery organization to lower business volumes and to increase the -efficiency. Restructuring charges increased to SEK &#150;3.0 (&#150;1.7) billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Professional Services operating income declined to SEK 5.2 (9.6) billion due to increased restructuring charges of SEK &#150;2.3 (&#150;0.7)
billion, lower sales and a negative impact from large projects in systems integration transformation, where operators are looking to transform their IT environments to increase efficiency and prepare for 5G. Ericsson has been successful and won
several IT transformation contracts. However, the short-term margin impact from these contracts is challenging as a consequence of investments in competence <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">build-up</FONT> and market share. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Network Rollout operating income declined to SEK &#150;1.9 (&#150;1.4) billion due to lower sales in combination with increased cost and
negative effects from a few contracts in emerging markets. The effort to improve Network Rollout -profitability continues through efficiency improvements including implementation of global methods and tools. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Support Solutions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Background </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Support Solutions represented 5.6% of net sales in 2016 (6.1% in 2015). The portfolio of Support Solutions is designed around measurable
performance improvements in an operator&#146;s business processes, with software that is scalable, configurable and that provides <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-to-end</FONT></FONT> capabilities. The business
segment develops and delivers software-based solutions for OSS and BSS as well as TV and media solutions.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Business in 2016 </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales as reported decreased by &#150;17%, partly due to lower IPR licensing revenues. OSS and BSS sales declined due to lower sales of legacy
products and lower software sales in digital transformation projects where sales are mainly project milestone based. In addition, sales declined in markets with a weak macroeconomic environment.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales in TV&nbsp;&amp; Media declined due to lower sales of legacy products primarily in North America. Customer trials on the next-generation
TV&nbsp;&amp; Media platform are ongoing, but have not yet translated into sales.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income declined to SEK &#150;1.0 (1.5) billion
mainly due to lower IPR licensing revenues and lower sales in both OSS and BSS as well as in TV&nbsp;&amp; Media. Several activities in order to reduce cost and adjust the organization to lower business volumes are ongoing. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The overall transition of business models -continues, from traditional telecom software licenses to recurrent license revenue deals. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business results &#150; Regions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">North
America </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">19 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mobile broadband investments were stable. Professional Services sales were negatively impacted by
reduced scope in a managed services contract. Support Solutions sales declined due to delayed investment decisions by customers. The focus on 5G strongly increased, with -trials ongoing with all major customers. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Latin America </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales decreased following
reduced mobile broadband investments due to a weak macroeconomic environment in the region and due to&nbsp;devaluation of local currencies. The strong momentum for digital transformation continued. Professional Services sales declined due to lower
activities in managed services. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Northern Europe and Central Asia </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined, primarily due to continued lower&nbsp;mobile broadband investments in Russia. Global Services sales were flat with a decline in
Network Rollout, offset by increased Managed Services sales in Sweden. OSS and BSS sales were flat while TV&nbsp;&amp; Media sales declined. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Western
and Central Europe </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined as the initial LTE deployments were finalized. Operators continue to focus on transforming their
networks to meet the increasing demand for coverage and capacity, while at the same time improving efficiency. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Mediterranean </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined due to lower investments in mobile broadband infrastructure, mainly related to capacity business. Operator investments in ICT
transformation and demand for managed services continued. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Middle East </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined, primarily in Networks due to lower broadband investments in Egypt, Pakistan, Ethiopia and Turkey. The decrease was partly
offset by growth in Global Services sales, mainly in network rollout and optimization services in Saudi Arabia. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Saharan</FONT> Africa </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Investments declined, impacted by a weak -macroeconomic environment, local currency depreciation in key markets as well as low oil
and&nbsp;commodity prices. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>India </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mobile broadband sales declined mainly driven by delayed spectrum auctions which delayed operator investments. Professional Services sales
remained stable with operators&#146; higher focus on network quality and cost optimization. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>North East Asia </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales declined slightly due to lower investments in Mainland China and Korea, partly offset by market share gains in Japan and Taiwan. In
Mainland China 4G deployments continued. However, reduced investments in legacy technologies and significantly reduced investment by&nbsp;one customer, impacted sales negatively.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>South East Asia and Oceania </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sales
increased, primarily driven by mobile broadband deployments across several markets. Professional Services sales developed favorably as operators focus on efficiency and network optimization services.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Other </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">IPR licensing revenues amounted to
SEK 10.0 (14.4) billion. Sales in 2015 were positively impacted by a global patent license agreement signed with Apple, which included an initial payment. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

of the 2017 Swedish Annual Report is incorporated herein by reference: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Note C20 &#150; Financial risk management and financial instruments </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
